04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 268: float G_GGX_Smith( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 269: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 270: 	float gl = dotNL + sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 272: 	return 1.0 / ( gl * gv );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 273: }
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 274: float G_GGX_SmithCorrelated( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 275: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 276: 	float gv = dotNL * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNV ) );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 277: 	float gl = dotNV * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 278: 	return 0.5 / max( gv + gl, EPSILON );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 279: }
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 280: float D_GGX( const in float alpha, const in float dotNH ) {

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 283: 	return RECIPROCAL_PI * a2 / pow2( denom );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 284: }

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 297: vec2 ltcTextureCoords( const in GeometricContext geometry, const in float roughness ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 298: 	const float LUT_SIZE  = 64.0;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 299: 	const float LUT_SCALE = (LUT_SIZE - 1.0)/LUT_SIZE;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 300: 	const float LUT_BIAS  = 0.5/LUT_SIZE;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 301: 	vec3 N = geometry.normal;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 302: 	vec3 V = geometry.viewDir;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 303: 	vec3 P = geometry.position;

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 308: 	uv = uv * LUT_SCALE + LUT_BIAS;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 309: 	return uv;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 310: }

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 387: 	return res;

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 397: 	vec3 V = geometry.viewDir;

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 416: 	clippedRect[4] = normalize( clippedRect[4] );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 417: 	float sum = 0.0;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 418: 	sum += integrateLtcBrdfOverRectEdge( clippedRect[0], clippedRect[1] );

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 459: vec3 BRDF_Specular_GGX_Environment( const in GeometricContext geometry, const in vec3 specularColor, const in float roughness ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 460: 	float dotNV = saturate( dot( geometry.normal, geometry.viewDir ) );

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 464: 	float a004 = min( r.x * r.x, exp2( - 9.28 * dotNV ) ) * r.x + r.y;

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 466: 	return specularColor * AB.x + AB.y;
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 467: }
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 468: float G_BlinnPhong_Implicit( ) {

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 471: float D_BlinnPhong( const in float shininess, const in float dotNH ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 472: 	return RECIPROCAL_PI * ( shininess * 0.5 + 1.0 ) * pow( dotNH, shininess );

04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 474: vec3 BRDF_Specular_BlinnPhong( const in IncidentLight incidentLight, const in GeometricContext geometry, const in vec3 specularColor, const in float shininess ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 475: 	vec3 halfDir = normalize( incidentLight.direction + geometry.viewDir );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 476: 	float dotNH = saturate( dot( geometry.normal, halfDir ) );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 477: 	float dotLH = saturate( dot( incidentLight.direction, halfDir ) );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 478: 	vec3 F = F_Schlick( specularColor, dotLH );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 479: 	float G = G_BlinnPhong_Implicit( );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 480: 	float D = D_BlinnPhong( shininess, dotNH );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 481: 	return F * ( G * D );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 482: }
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 483: float GGXRoughnessToBlinnExponent( const in float ggxRoughness ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 484: 	return ( 2.0 / pow2( ggxRoughness + 0.0001 ) - 2.0 );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 485: }
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 486: float BlinnExponentToGGXRoughness( const in float blinnExponent ) {
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 487: 	return sqrt( 2.0 / ( blinnExponent + 2.0 ) );
04-17 17:08:36.163 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 488: }

04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 748: 	vec2 cubeToUV( vec3 v, float texelSizeY ) {
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 749: 		vec3 absV = abs( v );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 750: 		float scaleToCube = 1.0 / max( absV.x, max( absV.y, absV.z ) );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 751: 		absV *= scaleToCube;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 752: 		v *= scaleToCube * ( 1.0 - 2.0 * texelSizeY );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 753: 		vec2 planar = v.xy;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 754: 		float almostATexel = 1.5 * texelSizeY;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 755: 		float almostOne = 1.0 - almostATexel;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 756: 		if ( absV.z >= almostOne ) {
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 757: 			if ( v.z > 0.0 )
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 758: 				planar.x = 4.0 - v.x;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 759: 		} else if ( absV.x >= almostOne ) {
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 760: 			float signX = sign( v.x );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 761: 			planar.x = v.z * signX + 2.0 * signX;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 762: 		} else if ( absV.y >= almostOne ) {
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 763: 			float signY = sign( v.y );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 764: 			planar.x = v.x + 2.0 * signY + 2.0;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 765: 			planar.y = v.z * signY - 2.0;
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 766: 		}
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 767: 		return vec2( 0.125, 0.25 ) * planar + vec2( 0.375, 0.75 );
04-17 17:08:36.164 13219 13241 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 768: 	}
